 Studies have reported that 80 percent of stress is caused by the workplace environment

 First of all, find out if you are in a state of stress, then find out the reason for stress
 kaarysthal main tanaav ke strot alag-alag ho sakate hai,kuch tanaav ke peeche karmchaariyon kii bhoomika hoti he to kuch nishchit peshey ke saath tanaav anivaary rup se judaa hota he or duusare tarah ke tanaav kaarysthal ke maahaul kii vajah se paidaa hote hai
 Stress arises due to unproductive facilities for employees or situations such as low wages in lieu of extra labor
 kaarysthal kaa kharaab maahaul,nirdhaarit samay par kaary puraa karne kaa dabaav aadi ke chalate bhi karmchaariyon kaa tanaav bad saktaa he
 Reasons that employees may face stress are: non-promotion, excessive accountability, being out of the decision-making process, employees' uncertainty about their position, disputes with peers, superiors or subordinates, their tasks Desperation arises from not being recognized, vague information about obligations, adverse workplace environment with stricter rules
 acchhee tarah vishleshan karne ke baad agar aapako aisa lagata he ki kaarysthal kii vajah se aap tanaav main rahete hai to khud ko tanaav mukt rakhane ke liye aap kuch sutara apana sakate hai
 - Find out what makes you feel stressed in your environment and consider your emotional and physical reaction
 yah samajhakar samasya ko nazarandaaj na karen ki yah aapane aap thik ho jayega
 Doing so can worsen the situation
 -apni bhaavnaatmak pratikriya kii saghanta ko kam karen
 Do not try to satisfy all the people around you
 apni praathamiktaayen nirdhaarit karen
 Understand that the tasks you do are not all important
 chizon ke sakaaratmak pahalu kii taraf dhyaan kendrit karen or nakaaratmak pahalu kii upeksha karen
 Use the meditation method to make the veins relaxed
 gahari saans lekar bhi swayan ko tanaav mukt rakhaa ja saktaa he
 Stress can also be kept away by practicing meditation for only 10 minutes daily
 -dhumrapaan or alcohol se dur rahen
 Consumption of cigarettes or alcohol increases stress rather than decreases

 One of my favourites!— Vijay Mallya (@thevijaymallya)june 11, 2016court se lagaai bhagoda ghoshit karne kii guharisase pehle pravartan nideshaalay (idi) ne mumbai ke vishesh piemele adaalat main arji dekar sharaab kaarobaari vijay maalya ko bhagoda ghoshit karne kii guhaar lagaai he
 ED is involved in money laundering investigation against Mallya in the bank loan scam case
 kai giraftaar warrant hai lambidhikariyon ne bataaya ki agency ne adaalat se aapraadhik dand prakriya samhita (siarpisi) kii dhara-82 ke tahat ek aadesh jari karne kaa aagrah kiya he
 Several arrest warrants are pending against Mallya, including the Non Bailable Warrant (NBW) under the Prevention of Money Laundering Act (PMLA)
 idi kii arji par adaalat 13 june ko aadesh de sakati he
 The agency has also informed the court about the status of its investigation and stated the need for Mallya to be involved in the investigation
 adhikari ne kaha ki agency ne mani londring virdohi adaalat se sampark saadhaa tha, jahaan semalyake khilaaf enbidblyoo jari hua tha
 The Supreme Court has denied early hearing by sending the matter to a five-judge constitution bench to consider the 1995 judgment on Hindutva and the issue of the use of religion in elections
 chif justise ranjan gogoi ne vakil salmaan khurshid kii us maang ko thukraayaa jisamen unhone kaha ki isaki paanch jajon kii samvidhan peeth main bhejkar jald sunwaayee ho
 At present, this issue is with the three judges' bench
 chif justise ne kaha ki aapaki najar main har cese ahm he, hamaari main nahin
 The court has its own priorities and they are different from yours
 darasal supreme court kii saat jajon kii samvidhan peeth ne 2 janvari 2017 ko ahm faisla dete hue kaha tha ki pratyaashee yaa uske samarthakon ke dharm, jati, samudaay, bhashaa ke naam par vot maangana gaiyrkanoonee he or ye karpt practice he
 a seven-judge bench of the Supreme Court once again made it clear that it was not going to re-examine the 1995 judgment in the Hindutva case
 iske baad 1995 hindutv jajment ko paanch jajon kii samvidhan peeth main bheja gaya
 The bench said that the reference sent by the five judges to seven judges was not Hinduism
 saat jajon ne reference dekar waapas paanch jajon kii bench ko bhej diya
 That is, the rest of the issues including Hindutva were to be heard by the same bench
 lekin ab supreme court main is mudde par paanch ke bajaae teen jajon kii peeth banaai gai he
 It is noteworthy that in December 1995, a bench of Justice JS Verma said that the word Hindutva refers to the lifestyle of the Indian people
 hindutv shabd ko sirf dharm tak simit nahin kiya ja saktaa
 According to Hindu culture, Kharmas expire after 14 January and the auspicious moment begins for everyone
 aise main bhartiya cricket team mangalvaar ko england ke saath khelte hue apane kharaab daur ko peeche chhodkar 'shubh vakt' main jeet ke safar kaa shubharambh karnaa chaahegi
 The Indian team is trailing 0–1 in the five-match ODI series
 kochi main vah jeet ke saath nai shuruyaat kar paaegi yaa nahin, yah to vakt hi batayega lekin beetaa ek maheenaa bharat ke liye behad kharaab rahaa he
 He lost in the Test series to England and then lost the ODI series to Pakistan
 rajkot main bharat ne 326 ranon ke vishaal lakshya kaa peechha karte hue 316 ran banaae the
 The match was important in many respects
 bade lakshya kaa peechha karte hue jeet ke itane kareeb pahunchakar usase maharoom rah janaa kharaab vakt kii ore ishaara karata he
 Now that Kharmas has passed, India faces new challenges
 use australia ke saath hone vaali gharelu test shrunkhlaa se pehle khud ko sambhaalanaa hoga or iske liye use english team par jeet hasil kerani hogi
 Captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni will have to avoid the mistakes he made in Rajkot
 shandaar farm main chal rahe cheteshwar pujaara ko antim ekadash main shaamil nahin karnaa dhoni ke liye aalochana kaa kaaran bana tha
 Dhoni could have included Pujara in the squad in place of Ravindra Jadeja but Jadeja, who performed all-round against Pakistan in the last match, got the captain's confidence and thus India had to go without a good in-form batsman
 
 dhoni ke liye yah vakt kharaab he
 There was a time when everything he used to touch would become gold, but today things have changed
 ek vakt aisa tha, jab dhoni ke galat faisle bhi sahi sabit ho jaaya karte the lekin aaj unke kai sahi faisle bhi galat sabit ho jaaya karte hai
 In such a situation, Dhoni should intentionally inspire his teammates to play well while avoiding any stubbornness or mistake
 yah team ke liye zyada jaruri he kyonki sachin tendulkar or virendra sahvaag ke bagaiyr team vaise bhi kamjor padati dikhaai de rahi he
 Moreover, the openers have not been able to give a good start on one occasion since last year
 team main pradarshan ke santulan kaa abhaav he
 That is why when bowlers do well, the batsmen flop and when the batsmen shine, the bowlers spoil the work
 rajkot main england ke teen ballebaajon ne 100 se adhik ausat se ran banaae the or bharat ke chaar ballebaaj isse adhik ausat se banane main safal rahe the lekin iske baavjood team haar gai thi
 The reason is simple, Indian batsmen will have to stay on the wicket for some more time
 yahi haal gendbaajon kaa he
 Ishant Sharma bowled brilliantly in the third match against Pakistan in Delhi but his 10-over quota at Rajkot scored 86 runs
 strike gendbaaj hone ke naate ishanth ko apane pradarshan main nirantarata lani hogi
 On the other hand, the English team has very few concerns with India
 uske ballebaaj acchhee lay main hai or gendbaaj bakhubi apana kaam kar rahe hai
 Despite losing the first two practice matches of the ODI series, the English team did not let their impact come on their performance
 captain elister cook dwaara ian bel ko salaami ballebaaj ke taur par aajmaana team ke liye nai urja ke sanchaar kaa kaaran bana he
 Since two practice matches, Bell has scored one century and two fifties so far
 tippaniyan He has good and in-form batsmen in the form of Eoin Morgan, Craig Keyswetter and Kevin Pietersen, who have the ability to score at a very fast pace
 in sabane rajkot main ise sabit bhi kiya he
 It is difficult to say what the Kochi pitch will do but it is so sure that the English team is looking to equalize the 5-0, 5-0 defeat in the last two series in India and it is very difficult to stop them in these conditions of India
 Will be difficult
 bhartiya team paanch maichon kii ekadivasiy shrunkhlaa main 0-1 se peeche chal rahi he
 Only time will tell whether she will be able to make a fresh start with a win in Kochi, but the last one month has been very bad for India
 use england ke haathon test shrunkhlaa main haar mili or phir pakistan ke haathon ekadivasiy shrunkhlaa ganvaani padi
 In Rajkot, India had scored 316 runs chasing a mammoth target of 326 runs
 vah match kai lihaaj se ahm tha
 Staying so close to victory while chasing a big goal indicates a bad time
 ab jabaki kharmaas biit chukaa he, bharat ke saamne nai chunautiyaan hai
 He has to manage himself before the home Test series with Australia and for that he will have to win over the English team
 captain mahendra singh dhoni ko un galatiyon se bachanaa hoga, jo unhone rajkot main kii thi
 The absence of the in-form Cheteshwar Pujara in the playing XI had caused criticism for Dhoni
 dhoni rabindra jadeja ke sthaan par pujaara ko team main shaamil kar sakate the lekin beete match main pakistan ke khilaaf harfanmaulaa pradarshan karne vaale jadeja ko captain kaa bharosa mila or is tarah bharat ko ek achche farm main chal rahe ballebaaj ke bina hi maidan main utarana padaa
 This time is bad for Dhoni
 ek samay tha, jab vah jis cheez ko choote the, sona ho jaataa tha lekin aaj halaat badal chuke hai
 There was a time when Dhoni's wrong decisions were also proved correct, but today many of his right decisions are also proved wrong
 aise main dhoni ko jaanboojhkar koi jid yaa galati se bachate hue apane saathiyon ko acha khilne ke liye prerit karnaa chahie
 This is more important for the team because without Sachin Tendulkar and Virender Sehwag, the team is seen to be weak anyway
 or to or salaami ballebaaj beete saal se lekar ab tak ek maukey par bhi acchhee shuruyaat nahin de sake hai
 The team lacks balance of performance
 yahi kaaran he jab gendbaaj acha karte hai to ballebaaj flop ho jate hai or jab ballebaaj chamakate hai to gendbaaj kaam kharaab kar dete hai
 In Rajkot, three England batsmen had scored more than 100 runs and four batsmen of India were able to make more than this average but despite this the team lost
 kaaran saaf he, bhartiya ballebaajon ko kuch or der tak wicket par tike rahanaa hoga
 It is the same for bowlers
 ishanth sharma ne pakistan ke khilaaf tisare mukaable main dilli main shandaar gendbaaji kii thi lekin rajkot main unke 10 over ke cote main 86 ran bane
 Being a strike bowler, Ishant has to be consistent in his performance
 duusari ore, english team ke saamne bharat se kaaphi kam chintaaen hai
 His batsmen are in good rhythm and the bowlers are doing their job well
 ekadivasiy shrunkhlaa se pehle do abhyaas match haarane ke baavjood english team ne uskaa asar apane pradarshan par nahin aane diya
 Trying Ian Bell as an opener by captain Alastair Cook has led to new energy communication for the team
 do abhyaas maichon se lekar ab tak bel ek shatak or do ardhshtak laga chuke hai
 The comments eon morgan, craig keeswaitor or kevin petersan ke rup main uske paas achche or farm main chal rahe ballebaaj hai, jo behad tej gati se ran banane kii kshamta rakhte hai
 They have all proved this in Rajkot
 kochi kii pich kya gul khilaaegi yah kahana mushkil he lekin itnaa jarur he ki english team bharat main beeti do shrunkhalaaon main mili 5-0, 5-0 kii haar kaa hisaab baraabar karne ko utaaru he or bharat ke in halaaton main use roak paanaa behad mushkil hoga

 5

 vakya tarantaaran jile ke bagiyadi gaanv kaa he

 Navdeep and Navpreet returned with Nirmal Singh on August 24 and asked for the rest
 sahib singh ne kaha ki uske paas paise nahin he

 jabaki donon bhai navdeep or navpreet abhi bhi faraar he

 anna jahaan andolan kaa elaan kar chuke hai, vahiin unke gharavaale anna kii sehat ko lekar phikrmand ho rahe hai
 The family members fear that Anna's health may not deteriorate during the fast
 anna ne 27 disambar ko ramlila maidan main phir se anshan par baithne kaa elaan to kar diya lekin unke gharavaalon ko unki sehat kii chintaa sata rahi he
 On the other hand, Anna's sister-in-law is also afraid that her health may deteriorate during the fast
 anna kii bhabhi kii maane to anna ziddee hai or wo jo thaan lete hai use puraa karke hi dam lete hai
 Let me tell you that two days ago, Anna's doctors also said that their health may be threatened during the fast
 lekin in sab baton kaa anna par asar hoga aisa nahin lagata
